  description varchar [note: 'Detailed description of the tier, including value proposition, benefits summary, and marketing messaging. Used in loyalty program communications and member portal.']
  downgrade_threshold decimal(12,2) [note: 'Minimum threshold value required to maintain this tier status during re-evaluation period. Falling below this value triggers downgrade to lower tier. Null indicates no downgrade policy.']
  early_access_lto boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members in this tier receive early access to new Limited Time Offers (LTO) before general availability. True if eligible, false otherwise.']
  effective_end_date date [note: 'Date when this tier configuration was retired or replaced. Null indicates the tier is currently active. Used for tier lifecycle management and historical analysis.']
  effective_start_date date [note: 'Date when this tier configuration became active and available for member assignment. Used for tier lifecycle management and historical analysis.']
  exclusive_offers_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members in this tier receive access to exclusive promotional offers and Limited Time Offers (LTO) not available to lower tiers. True if eligible, false otherwise.']
  free_delivery_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members in this tier are eligible for free delivery on Online Ordering (OLO) and Third-Party Delivery (3PD) orders. True if eligible, false otherwise.']
  grace_period_days varchar [note: 'Number of days after tier expiration during which members retain tier benefits before downgrade. Used to provide buffer period for re-qualification.']
  icon_url varchar [note: 'URL path to the tier badge or icon image asset used in member portal, mobile app, and digital communications. Supports tier visual identity and gamification.']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this tier record was last updated. Used for audit trail, change tracking, and data synchronization.']
  launch_date date [note: 'Date when this tier was officially launched to the market and communicated to guests. May differ from effective_start_date for soft launches or pilot programs.']
  max_redemption_discount_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Maximum percentage discount that can be applied when redeeming points for rewards in this tier (e.g., 20.00 for 20% max discount). Used to control reward economics and prevent abuse.']
  modified_by_user varchar [note: 'Username or identifier of the user who last modified this tier configuration. Used for audit trail and accountability.']
  name varchar [note: 'Human-readable display name of the loyalty tier (e.g., Bronze Member, Silver Member, Gold Member, Platinum Elite). Used in guest-facing communications and marketing materials.']
  points_multiplier decimal(5,2) [note: 'Multiplier applied to base points accrual for members in this tier (e.g., 1.0 for base, 1.5 for 50% bonus, 2.0 for double points). Used to calculate accelerated points earning.']
  priority_support_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members in this tier receive priority customer support (e.g., dedicated phone line, faster response times). True if eligible, false otherwise.']
  qualification_metric varchar [note: 'The metric used to determine tier qualification (points accrued, visit count, total spend amount, or transaction count). Defines how qualification_threshold is interpreted.']
  qualification_period_days varchar [note: 'Number of days over which the qualification threshold must be met (e.g., 365 for annual qualification, 90 for quarterly). Null indicates lifetime accumulation.']
  qualification_threshold decimal(12,2) [note: 'Numeric threshold value required to qualify for this tier (e.g., 1000 points, 25 visits, $500 spend). Interpretation depends on qualification_metric.']
  referral_bonus_points varchar [note: 'Bonus points awarded to members in this tier for each successful referral of a new loyalty program member. Used to incentivize member acquisition through word-of-mouth.']
  rollover_points_allowed boolean [note: 'Indicates whether unused points can roll over to the next qualification period for members in this tier. True if rollover is allowed, false if points expire at period end.']
  sort_order varchar [note: 'Integer defining the hierarchical display order of tiers (e.g., 1 for Bronze, 2 for Silver, 3 for Gold, 4 for Platinum). Lower values represent entry-level tiers; higher values represent premium tiers.']
  target_member_segment varchar [note: 'Description of the target guest segment this tier is designed to attract and retain (e.g., frequent visitors, high spenders, digital-first guests, family diners). Used for marketing strategy and program design.']
  tier_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the tier. Active tiers are available for member assignment; inactive tiers are temporarily disabled; retired tiers are no longer offered but may have legacy members; pending tiers are configured but not yet launched.']
  upgrade_notification boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members should receive automated notification when they qualify for upgrade to this tier. True if notification is enabled, false otherwise.']
  validity_days varchar [note: 'Number of days a member retains this tier status after qualification before re-evaluation (e.g., 365 for annual renewal). Null indicates permanent tier assignment.']
  welcome_bonus_points varchar [note: 'One-time bonus points awarded to a member upon first achieving this tier. Used to incentivize tier progression and enhance member engagement.']

  Note: 'Reference catalog of all loyalty membership tiers (e.g., Bronze, Silver, Gold, Platinum) defined in the Restaurants loyalty program. Stores tier name, tier code, qualification threshold (points or visit count), tier benefits summary, tier multiplier for points accrual, tier validity period, and sort order. Drives tier assignment logic and benefit entitlement across the program.'
}

Table loyalty.points_ledger {
  points_ledger_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for each points transaction record in the loyalty ledger. Serves as the immutable primary key for this financial-grade system of record.']
  accrual_rule_id decimal(18,2) [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.accrual_rule. Business justification: points_ledger is the financial-grade immutable record of every points movement. For accrual entries, the specific accrual_rule that governed the points calculation (rate, multiplier, eligibility) shou']
  loyalty_member_id varchar [note: 'Unique identifier of the loyalty program member whose points balance is affected by this transaction. Links to the member master record.']
  offer_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.offer. Business justification: points_ledger records every points movement including bonus points triggered by offer redemptions (e.g., double-points offers, bonus point campaigns). Without an offer_id FK, there is no way to trace ']
  points_restaurant_unit_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the restaurant location where this points transaction originated. Populated for POS and kiosk transactions. Null for OLO, mobile app, or admin transactions not tied to a specific physical location.']
  pos_terminal_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to restaurant.pos_terminal. Business justification: Points are earned at a specific POS terminal during a transaction. POS-level points accrual auditing, fraud detection, and terminal reconciliation reports require knowing which terminal processed each']
  primary_points_adjusted_by_user_employee_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the system user or customer service agent who authorized and executed the manual adjustment or reversal. Populated for adjust and reversal transactions. Critical for SOX compliance and fraud prevention.']
  primary_points_guest_order_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the originating order transaction that triggered this points movement. Populated for earn and redeem transactions tied to guest purchases. Null for non-order events such as bonus awards, expirations, or manual adjustments.']
  reversal_of_transaction_points_ledger_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the original points_ledger_id that this reversal transaction is canceling. Populated only for reversal transaction types. Creates an audit chain linking reversals to their source transactions.']
  reward_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the specific reward item redeemed by the member. Populated only for redeem transaction types. Links to the rewards catalog to identify what was claimed (free item, discount, experience).']
  source_transaction_guest_order_id varchar [note: 'The unique transaction identifier from the originating source system. Enables end-to-end traceability and reconciliation between the loyalty ledger and upstream systems. Format varies by source system.']
  tier_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the loyalty membership tier the member held at the time of this transaction. Used to determine earn rates, bonus multipliers, and redemption privileges. Links to tier master data.']
  adjustment_reason_code varchar [note: 'Standardized code explaining why a manual adjustment or reversal was made. Populated only for adjust and reversal transaction types. Supports audit compliance and customer service quality tracking.']
  adjustment_reason_notes varchar [note: 'Free-text explanation provided by the customer service representative or system administrator who initiated the adjustment. Populated for adjust and reversal transactions. Supports audit trail and dispute resolution.']
  batch_reference varchar [note: 'Identifier of the processing batch or job that created this ledger entry. Used for bulk operations such as nightly expiration runs, mass bonus awards, or system migrations. Null for real-time individual transactions.']
  fiscal_period varchar [note: 'The fiscal period (month or accounting period number) within the fiscal year when this transaction occurred. Supports monthly financial close, P&L reporting, and loyalty liability accrual tracking.']
  fiscal_year varchar [note: 'The fiscal year in which this points transaction occurred, derived from transaction_timestamp. Supports financial reporting, GAAP revenue recognition for breakage, and year-over-year loyalty program analytics.']
  is_voided boolean [note: 'Flag indicating whether this transaction has been voided or reversed by a subsequent transaction. True if a reversal exists, false otherwise. Immutable ledger entries are never deleted, only marked as voided.']
  order_currency_code varchar [note: 'Three-letter ISO 4217 currency code for the order total amount. Supports multi-currency loyalty programs for international operations. Null for non-order transactions.']
  order_total_amount decimal(15,2) [note: 'The total monetary value of the order that triggered this points transaction, in the local currency. Used to calculate points earn rate and for financial reconciliation. Null for non-order transactions.']
  points_balance_after decimal(18,2) [note: 'The cumulative running balance of points for this member immediately after this transaction was applied. Provides audit trail and reconciliation capability. Must equal prior balance plus points_delta.']
  points_delta varchar [note: 'The signed integer change in points balance for this transaction. Positive values represent accruals (earn, bonus), negative values represent deductions (redeem, expire, adjust downward). Zero-delta entries are not permitted.']
  points_earn_rate decimal(10,4) [note: 'The rate at which points were earned per currency unit spent. Example: 1.0000 means 1 point per dollar, 2.0000 means 2 points per dollar (double points promotion). Populated for earn transactions, null otherwise.']
  points_expiry_date date [note: 'The date on which the points earned in this transaction will expire if not redeemed. Populated only for earn and bonus transaction types. Null for redeem, expire, and adjust transactions. Supports FIFO expiration logic and member communication.']
  processed_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this ledger entry was committed to the loyalty system of record. May differ from transaction_timestamp for batch processing or delayed reconciliation. Used for ETL audit and SLA monitoring.']
  restaurant_number varchar [note: 'Human-readable store or unit number for the restaurant location. Denormalized for operational reporting and guest service. Null for non-location-specific transactions.']
  source_channel varchar [note: 'The originating channel or interface through which this points transaction was initiated: POS (Point of Sale in-store), OLO (Online Ordering web platform), mobile_app (native mobile application), kiosk (self-service in-store kiosk), 3PD (Third-Party Delivery partner), call_center (phone order), admin (manual back-office adjustment). [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: pos|olo|mobile_app|kiosk|3pd|call_center|admin — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  source_order_number varchar [note: 'Human-readable order number or receipt identifier from the POS or OLO system. Provides guest-facing reference for customer service inquiries. Null for non-order transactions.']
  source_system_code varchar [note: 'Code identifying the operational system that originated this points transaction. Supports multi-system integration and data lineage tracking. Examples: micros_pos (Oracle MICROS POS), olo_platform (Olo Digital Ordering), salesforce_crm (Salesforce Marketing Cloud), loyalty_engine (core loyalty platform), admin_portal (back-office admin tool).']
  transaction_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The precise date and time when this points transaction occurred in the source system. Represents the business event time, not the ETL load time. Critical for sequencing and audit.']
  transaction_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the points movement: earn (points accrued from purchase or activity), redeem (points spent on rewards), expire (points lapsed due to inactivity or time limit), adjust (manual correction by support or system), bonus (promotional award), reversal (cancellation of prior transaction).']
  voided_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this transaction was voided by a reversal. Null if the transaction has not been voided. Supports audit trail and reconciliation.']

  Note: 'Immutable financial-grade ledger recording every points movement for a loyalty member — accruals, redemptions, expirations, adjustments, bonus awards, goodwill credits, promotional credits, dispute resolutions, system error corrections, and fraud reversals. Each row captures transaction type (earn, redeem, expire, adjust, bonus, goodwill, reversal, correction), points delta, running balance, source channel (POS, OLO, 3PD), source order reference, campaign reference, expiry date of earned points, adjustment reason code, adjustment category (goodwill, dispute, error_correction, promotional, fraud), authorizing agent (for manual adjustments), approval status (auto_approved, pending_review, approved, rejected), processing timestamp, and related original transaction reference (for reversals/corrections). This is the single SSOT for ALL member point balance movements — no other product in this domain records points changes of any kind.'
}

Table loyalty.reward {
  reward_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty reward. Primary key.']
  brand_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to restaurant.brand. Business justification: Rewards (free items, discounts) are brand-specific — a reward valid at Brand A cannot be redeemed at Brand B. Brand-level reward catalog management and redemption cost accounting require this FK. The ']
  created_by_employee_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to workforce.employee. Business justification: Reward catalog management requires tracking which employee created each reward for audit, accountability, and content governance. The existing created_by plain-text field is denormalized; this FK enab']
  free_combo_meal_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to menu.combo_meal. Business justification: Combo Meal Reward Fulfillment: rewards frequently grant free combo meals (a distinct product from menu_item). POS and OLO systems must resolve which combo_meal_id to fulfill. Role-prefix \'free_combo_m']
  menu_item_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific menu item associated with this reward (for food and beverage rewards). Links to the menu item master catalog. Null for non-menu rewards.']
  modifier_group_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to menu.modifier_group. Business justification: Modifier Upgrade Reward: a common restaurant loyalty reward type grants a free modifier upgrade (e.g., free size upgrade, free add-on). The POS must resolve which modifier_group the reward applies to.']
  program_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.program. Business justification: Rewards in the catalog belong to a specific loyalty program — points costs, redemption rules, and availability are program-specific. Without program_id on reward, the reward catalog cannot be scoped t']
  stock_item_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to inventory.stock_item. Business justification: When a loyalty reward is a free menu item, the kitchen and inventory system must know which stock_item to pull and decrement. This FK enables COGS tracking for free-item rewards and inventory deductio']
  availability_end_date date [note: 'Date when this reward is no longer available for redemption. Null for evergreen rewards with no expiration. Used for Limited Time Offer (LTO) rewards and seasonal promotions.']
  availability_start_date date [note: 'Date when this reward becomes available for redemption by loyalty members. Used for Limited Time Offer (LTO) rewards and seasonal promotions.']
  code varchar [note: 'Externally-known unique alphanumeric code for the reward, used in Point of Sale (POS) and Online Ordering (OLO) systems for redemption lookup.']
  combinable_with_other_offers boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this reward can be combined with other promotional offers, coupons, or discounts in a single transaction. True if combinable, False if exclusive.']
  cost_of_goods_sold decimal(10,2) [note: 'Direct cost to the business to fulfill this reward, including food cost, packaging, and direct labor. Used for profitability analysis, loyalty program Return on Investment (ROI) calculation, and financial accrual. Expressed in USD.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this reward record was first created in the system. Used for audit trail and data lineage tracking.']
  daypart_restriction varchar [note: 'Specifies which daypart(s) this reward can be redeemed during: breakfast, lunch, dinner, late night, or all day. Used to manage product mix (PMIX) and drive traffic during specific service periods.']
  description varchar [note: 'Detailed description of the reward, including terms, conditions, and guest-facing messaging used in marketing materials and the loyalty app.']
  discount_type varchar [note: 'Type of discount mechanism applied: percentage (e.g., 10% off), fixed amount (e.g., $5 off), free item (no charge), buy-one-get-one (BOGO), or none (for non-discount rewards like merchandise or experiences).']
  discount_value decimal(10,2) [note: 'Numeric value of the discount. For percentage discounts, this is the percentage (e.g., 15.00 for 15%). For fixed amount discounts, this is the dollar amount (e.g., 5.00 for $5 off). Null for free items and non-discount rewards.']
  featured_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this reward is featured prominently in the loyalty app and marketing campaigns. True if featured, False if standard catalog placement. Used to drive awareness and redemption of strategic rewards.']
  format_restriction_list varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of restaurant format types where this reward is valid (e.g., QSR, casual, fine-dining, food court). Null if applicable to all formats. Used when restaurant_applicability_scope is \'specific_formats\'.']
  image_url varchar [note: 'URL path to the reward image asset displayed in the loyalty app, Online Ordering (OLO) platform, and marketing materials. Used for visual merchandising and guest engagement.']
  market_restriction_list varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of market codes or geographic regions where this reward is valid. Null if applicable to all markets. Used when restaurant_applicability_scope is \'specific_markets\'.']
  minimum_purchase_amount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Minimum transaction amount required to redeem this reward. Null if no minimum purchase is required. Used to protect Average Check Value (ACV) and prevent low-value transactions.']
  modified_by varchar [note: 'User identifier or system account that last modified this reward record. Used for audit trail and accountability.']
  modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this reward record was last modified. Used for audit trail, change tracking, and data synchronization across systems.']
  monetary_value decimal(10,2) [note: 'Estimated dollar value equivalent of the reward for financial reporting, liability accrual, and Average Check Value (ACV) impact analysis. Expressed in USD.']
  name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name of the reward displayed to guests in the loyalty app, Online Ordering (OLO) platform, and Point of Sale (POS) system.']
  partner_name varchar [note: 'Name of the third-party partner providing this reward (for partner offers). Null for internally-fulfilled rewards. Used for co-branded rewards and strategic partnerships.']
  partner_offer_code varchar [note: 'External offer code or voucher code provided by the partner for redemption tracking. Null for internally-fulfilled rewards.']
  points_cost decimal(18,2) [note: 'Number of loyalty points required to redeem this reward. Used to calculate point liability and drive guest engagement.']
  quantity_limit_per_member varchar [note: 'Maximum number of times a single loyalty member can redeem this reward during the availability window. Null indicates no limit.']
  redemption_channel_app boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this reward can be redeemed exclusively through the branded mobile app (distinct from general OLO). True if eligible, False if not.']
  redemption_channel_drive_thru boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this reward can be redeemed at Drive-Thru (DT) service points. True if eligible, False if not.']
  redemption_channel_olo boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this reward can be redeemed through Online Ordering (OLO) platforms including web and mobile app. True if eligible, False if not.']
  redemption_channel_pos boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this reward can be redeemed at Point of Sale (POS) terminals in restaurant locations. True if eligible, False if not.']
  redemption_channel_third_party_delivery boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this reward can be redeemed through Third-Party Delivery (3PD) platforms such as DoorDash, Uber Eats, or Grubhub. True if eligible, False if not.']
  redemption_count varchar [note: 'Total number of times this reward has been redeemed by loyalty members since inception. Used for popularity analysis, inventory planning, and loyalty program performance reporting.']
  restaurant_applicability_scope varchar [note: 'Defines which restaurant units can honor this reward: all units (system-wide), specific markets (geographic regions), specific formats (Quick-Service Restaurant (QSR), casual, fine-dining), franchise only, or company-owned only.']
  reward_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the reward: active (available for redemption), inactive (temporarily unavailable), pending (scheduled for future activation), expired (past availability end date), or discontinued (permanently removed from catalog).']
  reward_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the reward by category: food item (free menu item), beverage (free drink), discount (percentage or dollar off), merchandise (branded goods), experience (event access, VIP treatment), or partner offer (third-party rewards).']
  tax_treatment varchar [note: 'Indicates how sales tax is applied to this reward: taxable (tax calculated on reward value), non-taxable (no tax applied), or tax included (tax already embedded in points cost). Required for accurate Point of Sale (POS) processing and financial reporting.']
  terms_and_conditions varchar [note: 'Legal terms and conditions governing the redemption and use of this reward. Includes restrictions, exclusions, and compliance language required by Federal Trade Commission (FTC) regulations.']
  tier_eligibility varchar [note: 'Specifies which loyalty membership tier(s) are eligible to redeem this reward. Used to create tier-exclusive rewards that drive tier progression and engagement.']
  total_quantity_limit decimal(18,2) [note: 'Maximum total number of redemptions allowed across all loyalty members for this reward. Used for limited-supply rewards and exclusive experiences. Null indicates no limit.']

  Note: 'Master catalog of all redeemable rewards available in the Restaurants loyalty rewards catalog — free menu items, discounts, merchandise, experiences, and partner offers. Captures reward name, reward type (food, discount, merchandise, experience), points cost, monetary value equivalent, redemption channel eligibility (POS, OLO, app), availability window (start/end date), quantity limit, restaurant applicability scope (all units, specific markets, specific formats), and active status. Distinct from promotional offers which are push-based incentives.'
}

Table loyalty.redemption {
  redemption_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty reward redemption transaction. Primary key.']
  employee_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the employee who processed the redemption transaction at the POS, if applicable to in-store redemptions.']
  guest_order_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the order transaction where the reward was applied and redeemed.']
  member_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the loyalty program member who redeemed the reward.']
  menu_item_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific menu item that was redeemed or discounted through this reward, if applicable to item-specific rewards.']
  pos_terminal_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the POS terminal or kiosk device where the redemption was processed, sourced from Oracle MICROS POS system.']
  redeemed_combo_meal_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to menu.combo_meal. Business justification: Combo Meal Redemption Tracking: when a loyalty reward for a combo meal is redeemed, operations and finance need to track which combo_meal was fulfilled for PMIX reporting and food cost reconciliation.']
  redemption_restaurant_unit_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the restaurant unit where the redemption occurred.']
  redemption_unit_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the restaurant unit where the redemption occurred.']
  reward_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific reward item redeemed from the loyalty rewards catalog.']
  channel varchar [note: 'The customer-facing channel through which the reward was redeemed. POS (Point of Sale) for in-store counter, OLO (Online Ordering) for web ordering, mobile app for native app, kiosk for self-service terminal, drive-thru for drive-through window, third-party delivery for 3PD platforms.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this redemption record was first created in the loyalty system.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'Three-letter ISO 4217 currency code for the discount amount (e.g., USD, EUR, GBP).']
  daypart varchar [note: 'The time-of-day segment when the redemption occurred, used for analyzing redemption patterns by service period.']
  discount_amount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Monetary discount value applied to the order as a result of the reward redemption, in local currency.']
  expiration_date date [note: 'Date on which the redeemed reward was set to expire if not used, relevant for tracking near-expiry redemption behavior.']
  fraud_flag boolean [note: 'Boolean indicator set to true if the redemption was flagged for potential fraudulent activity or policy violation.']
  fraud_score decimal(5,2) [note: 'Numeric fraud risk score assigned by the loyalty platform fraud detection engine, ranging from 0.00 (low risk) to 100.00 (high risk).']
  fulfillment_code varchar [note: 'Alphanumeric confirmation code generated upon successful fulfillment of the redemption, used for audit and reconciliation.']
  member_tier varchar [note: 'Loyalty program membership tier of the member at the time of redemption, used for tier-based redemption analysis.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text notes or comments captured by the employee or system regarding special circumstances or issues with the redemption.']
  order_total_after_discount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Total order amount after the loyalty reward discount was applied, representing the net revenue from the transaction.']
  order_total_before_discount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Total order amount before the loyalty reward discount was applied, used for calculating incremental ACV (Average Check Value) impact.']
  points_balance_after decimal(18,2) [note: 'Loyalty points balance of the member immediately after this redemption transaction.']
  points_balance_before decimal(18,2) [note: 'Loyalty points balance of the member immediately before this redemption transaction.']
  points_deducted varchar [note: 'Number of loyalty points deducted from the member account to redeem this reward.']
  redemption_number varchar [note: 'Externally visible unique business identifier for the redemption transaction, used for customer service and tracking.']
  redemption_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the redemption transaction. Pending indicates awaiting fulfillment, fulfilled indicates successfully applied, voided indicates cancelled before fulfillment, expired indicates reward expired before use, reversed indicates post-fulfillment reversal, failed indicates technical or validation failure.']
  redemption_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the loyalty member initiated the reward redemption at the point of sale or online ordering platform.']
  reversal_reason varchar [note: 'Free-text explanation for why the redemption was reversed or voided, captured for customer service and fraud analysis.']
  reversal_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the redemption was reversed or voided, if applicable.']
  reward_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the reward redeemed. Discount for percentage or fixed amount off, free item for complimentary menu item, BOGO (Buy One Get One) for promotional offer, upgrade for size or quality enhancement, combo deal for bundled offer, birthday reward for member birthday incentive.']
  source varchar [note: 'Indicates how the redemption was initiated. Manual for member-selected reward, automatic for system-applied offer, promotional trigger for campaign-driven redemption, gamification for achievement-based reward, tier benefit for membership tier perk.']
  third_party_delivery_partner varchar [note: 'Name of the third-party delivery platform if the redemption occurred through a 3PD channel (e.g., DoorDash, Uber Eats, Grubhub).']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this redemption record was last modified in the loyalty system.']

  Note: 'Transactional record of every burn event by a loyalty member — both reward catalog redemptions (member-initiated pull from rewards catalog) and offer redemptions (program-initiated push incentives). Captures member reference, redemption type (reward, offer), reward or offer reference, redemption channel (POS, OLO, drive-thru, kiosk), restaurant unit, order reference, redemption timestamp, points deducted, monetary discount applied, offer assignment reference (for offer-type), delivery confirmation details, redemption status (pending, fulfilled, voided, expired, duplicate_attempt), and fulfillment confirmation. Unified SSOT for ALL burn events — no other product in this domain records redemption transactions. Enables holistic redemption analytics, PMIX impact analysis, offer ROI measurement, and reward popularity tracking.'
}

Table loyalty.accrual_rule {
  accrual_rule_id decimal(18,2) [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty points accrual rule. Primary key.']
  approved_by_employee_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to workforce.employee. Business justification: Loyalty accrual rule approval is a compliance and change-management process requiring an auditable link to the approving employee. The existing approved_by plain-text field is denormalized; this FK en']
  brand_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to restaurant.brand. Business justification: Accrual rules are scoped to specific brands in multi-brand enterprises. Brand managers need to query which earning rules apply to their brand for loyalty cost reporting and P&L attribution. No existin']
  program_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.program. Business justification: Accrual rules belong to a specific loyalty program; linking accrual_rule to program enables program‑level governance of rules.']
  approved_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this accrual rule was approved for activation. Null for draft or unapproved rules. Part of governance audit trail.']
  channel_scope varchar [note: 'Order channel(s) where this accrual rule is active. All = applies across all channels, POS = Point of Sale (Point of Sale) in-store, OLO = Online Ordering (Online Ordering) web/app, Mobile_app = native mobile application, Kiosk = self-service kiosk, Drive_thru = drive-through lane, 3PD = Third-Party Delivery (Third-Party Delivery) platforms. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: all|pos|olo|mobile_app|kiosk|drive_thru|3pd — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this accrual rule record was first created in the system. Part of audit trail.']
  daypart_scope varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of daypart codes (e.g., breakfast, lunch, dinner, late_night) to which this rule applies. Empty or null = applies to all dayparts. Used for time-of-day promotional earning.']
  earning_basis varchar [note: 'The calculation basis for points accrual. Dollar_spent = points per currency unit, Transaction_count = points per visit, Item_count = points per menu item purchased, Fixed_event = flat points for qualifying event.']
  effective_end_date date [note: 'Date when this accrual rule expires and stops awarding points. Null = no expiration (evergreen rule). Part of the rule\'s validity period.']
  effective_start_date date [note: 'Date when this accrual rule becomes active and begins awarding points. Part of the rule\'s validity period.']
  exclusion_list varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of menu item codes, categories, or member segments explicitly excluded from this rule. Used to carve out exceptions (e.g., alcohol, gift cards, discounted items).']
  fixed_points_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Flat number of points awarded for qualifying events (e.g., 500 points for birthday, 100 points for survey completion). Used when earning_basis is fixed_event. Null for variable earning rules.']
  franchise_id_list varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of franchisee IDs when franchise_scope is specific_franchisee. Null for all other franchise scopes.']
  franchise_scope varchar [note: 'Ownership model scope for this rule. All = applies to all restaurants, Company_owned = corporate locations only, Franchise = franchisee locations only, Specific_franchisee = limited to designated franchisee IDs (stored in franchise_id_list).']
  geographic_scope varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of country codes, region codes, or restaurant location codes where this rule is active. Empty or null = applies globally. Used for market-specific promotions.']
  maximum_points_per_day varchar [note: 'Cap on the number of points a member can earn per calendar day under this rule. Null = no daily cap. Used for frequency-based earning controls.']
  maximum_points_per_member varchar [note: 'Lifetime or campaign-period cap on points a single member can earn under this rule. Null = no member cap. Used for limited-time offers and promotional campaigns.']
  maximum_points_per_transaction varchar [note: 'Cap on the number of points that can be earned in a single transaction under this rule. Null = no cap. Used to prevent abuse and manage liability.']
  member_tier_scope varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of loyalty tier codes (e.g., bronze, silver, gold, platinum) eligible for this rule. Empty or null = applies to all tiers. Used for tier-exclusive earning opportunities.']
  menu_category_scope varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of menu category codes to which this rule applies. Empty or null = applies to all categories. Used to restrict earning to specific product categories (e.g., beverages, entrees, LTO items).']
  menu_item_scope varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of specific menu item codes to which this rule applies. Empty or null = applies to all items within category scope. Used for item-specific promotions.']
  minimum_purchase_amount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Minimum transaction subtotal required to qualify for this accrual rule. Null = no minimum threshold. Used for spend-tier promotions.']
  modified_by varchar [note: 'User ID or system identifier of the person or process that last modified this accrual rule. Used for audit trail and accountability.']
  modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this accrual rule record was last updated. Part of audit trail for change tracking.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text field for additional business context, implementation notes, or special instructions related to this accrual rule. Used by loyalty program managers for operational documentation.']
  points_expiration_days decimal(9,4) [note: 'Number of days from earning date after which points awarded by this rule expire. Null = points do not expire. Used for promotional points with limited validity.']
  points_per_unit decimal(10,2) [note: 'Number of loyalty points awarded per unit of the earning basis (e.g., 10 points per dollar spent, 50 points per transaction). Null for fixed_event earning basis.']
  requires_opt_in boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members must explicitly opt in or activate this rule to earn points. True = member action required, False = automatically applied to eligible transactions.']
  rule_code varchar [note: 'Business-readable unique code for the accrual rule (e.g., BASE_EARN, TIER_BONUS, BIRTHDAY_PROMO). Used for operational reference and system integration.']
  rule_description varchar [note: 'Detailed description of the accrual rule, including business logic, conditions, and intended use case.']
  rule_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name of the accrual rule for display and reporting purposes.']
  rule_priority varchar [note: 'Numeric priority for conflict resolution when multiple accrual rules apply to the same transaction. Lower number = higher priority. Used to determine which rule takes precedence (e.g., promotional rule overrides base earning).']
  rule_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of the accrual rule. Draft = under development, Active = currently awarding points, Paused = temporarily disabled, Expired = past effective_end_date, Archived = retired and no longer in use.']
  rule_type varchar [note: 'Category of earning trigger that activates this accrual rule. Purchase = transaction-based earning, Visit = frequency-based earning, Referral = member-get-member, Birthday = anniversary reward, Survey = feedback incentive, Signup = enrollment bonus.']
  stackable boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this rule can be combined with other accrual rules in the same transaction. True = can stack with other rules, False = mutually exclusive (highest priority rule wins).']
  tier_multiplier_applicable decimal(18,2) [note: 'Indicates whether member tier multipliers (e.g., Gold = 1.5x, Platinum = 2x) apply to this accrual rule. True = tier bonus applies, False = base earning only.']
  version_number varchar [note: 'Version number of this accrual rule for change tracking and auditability. Incremented each time the rule is modified. Supports rule versioning and rollback.']
  created_by varchar [note: 'User ID or system identifier of the person or process that created this accrual rule. Used for audit trail and accountability.']

  Note: 'Business rules governing how loyalty points are earned across channels, dayparts, menu categories, and member tiers. Each rule defines the earning trigger (purchase, visit, referral, birthday, survey), points awarded per dollar spent or per qualifying event, applicable tier multipliers, menu item or category scope, channel scope (POS, OLO, 3PD), effective date range, and rule priority for conflict resolution. Managed by the loyalty program team and versioned for auditability.'
}

Table loyalty.offer {
  offer_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty offer. Primary key.']
  brand_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to restaurant.brand. Business justification: Offers are created and governed by specific restaurant brands in a multi-brand portfolio. Brand marketing teams manage offer catalogs per brand for campaign planning and promotional ROI reporting. No ']
  created_by_employee_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to workforce.employee. Business justification: Links each promotional offer to the employee who created it, supporting audit trails, attribution, and marketing performance analysis.']
  free_item_menu_item_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to menu.menu_item. Business justification: Free Item Offer Fulfillment: when a loyalty offer grants a free specific menu item, the POS/OLO system must resolve the exact menu_item_id to apply the discount. free_item_sku is a denormalized refere']
  menu_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to menu.menu. Business justification: Menu-Scoped Offer Configuration: loyalty offers are scoped to specific menus (e.g., breakfast menu, digital menu, franchise menu). Marketing and operations teams configure and report on which menu an ']
  program_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.program. Business justification: Offers are scoped to a specific loyalty program — a Bronze/Silver/Gold offer structure for Program A is distinct from Program B\'s offers. Without program_id on offer, there is no way to filter or asso']
  stock_item_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to inventory.stock_item. Business justification: Promotional offers with a free item (e.g., \'free fries with purchase\') require inventory planning — operations must know which stock_item to pre-position and how much to order. This FK links the offer']
  supplier_contract_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to supply.supplier_contract. Business justification: Supplier-funded promotional offers (e.g., bonus points on a supplier\'s featured product) are governed by a supplier contract specifying funding terms, redemption caps, and reimbursement. This FK enabl']
  approved_by_user varchar [note: 'Username or user ID of the marketing manager who approved the offer for distribution. Null if offer is still in draft status.']
  approved_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the offer was approved for distribution. Null if offer is still in draft status.']
  auto_apply_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the offer is automatically applied at checkout when eligibility criteria are met (True) or requires manual code entry by the member (False).']
  bonus_points_value decimal(18,2) [note: 'Number of bonus loyalty points awarded when the offer is redeemed. Applicable to bonus_points and challenge offer types. Null for other offer types.']
  code varchar [note: 'Externally-visible unique alphanumeric code used by members to redeem the offer at POS or OLO channels. Typically 6-12 characters.']
  created_by_user varchar [note: 'Username or user ID of the marketing team member who created the offer in Salesforce CRM.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the offer record was first created in the Salesforce CRM system.']
  day_of_week_restriction varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of days of the week when the offer is valid (e.g., monday,tuesday,wednesday). Null if valid all days.']
  daypart_restriction varchar [note: 'Daypart(s) during which the offer is valid: breakfast, lunch, dinner, late_night, all_day. Null if no daypart restriction applies.']
  description varchar [note: 'Detailed marketing copy describing the offer terms, benefits, and redemption instructions displayed to members.']
  discount_type varchar [note: 'Mechanism of discount for discount-type offers: percentage (e.g., 20% off), fixed_amount (e.g., $5 off), free_item (specific SKU at no charge). Null for non-discount offer types.']
  discount_value decimal(10,2) [note: 'Numeric value of the discount: percentage (e.g., 20.00 for 20%), dollar amount (e.g., 5.00 for $5 off), or 0 for free_item offers. Null for non-discount offer types.']
  eligible_member_segments varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of member segment codes targeted for this offer (e.g., lapsed_guests, high_frequency, new_members). Null if offer is mass-distributed.']
  eligible_member_tiers varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of loyalty membership tier codes eligible to receive this offer (e.g., silver, gold, platinum). Null if offer is available to all tiers.']
  eligible_menu_items varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of menu item SKUs or category codes that qualify for the offer. Null if offer applies to entire menu or transaction total.']
  end_date date [note: 'Date when the offer expires and is no longer redeemable. Null for evergreen offers without a fixed expiration.']
  estimated_cost_per_redemption decimal(10,2) [note: 'Estimated financial cost to the business for each redemption of this offer, including discount value and incremental COGS. Used for campaign budget planning and ROI analysis.']
  excluded_menu_items varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of menu item SKUs or category codes explicitly excluded from the offer (e.g., alcohol, LTO items). Null if no exclusions.']
  geographic_restriction varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of geographic region codes, market codes, or restaurant IDs where the offer is valid. Null if valid at all locations.']
  image_url varchar [note: 'URL to the promotional image or banner displayed with the offer in mobile app, email, and digital channels.']
  minimum_purchase_amount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Minimum transaction subtotal (before tax) required to qualify for the offer. Null if no minimum purchase requirement.']
  minimum_visit_frequency varchar [note: 'Minimum number of visits in the trailing 90 days required for a member to be eligible for this offer. Null if no visit frequency requirement.']
  modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the offer record was last modified in the Salesforce CRM system.']
  name varchar [note: 'Marketing name of the offer displayed to loyalty members in app, email, and push notifications.']
  offer_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of the offer: draft (being designed), scheduled (approved, awaiting start date), active (live and redeemable), paused (temporarily suspended), expired (end date passed), cancelled (terminated before expiration).']
  offer_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the offer mechanism: discount (percentage or dollar off), bonus_points (accelerated points accrual), free_item (complimentary menu item), bogo (buy-one-get-one), challenge (gamification task), sweepstakes (prize drawing entry).']
  points_multiplier decimal(5,2) [note: 'Multiplier applied to base points accrual during the offer period (e.g., 2.00 for double points, 3.00 for triple points). Applicable to bonus_points offers. Null for other offer types.']
  priority_rank varchar [note: 'Display priority ranking for this offer when multiple offers are available to a member. Lower numbers indicate higher priority (1 = highest).']
  redemption_channel varchar [note: 'Channel(s) where the offer can be redeemed: pos (in-store point of sale), olo (online ordering), mobile_app, kiosk, drive_thru, all_channels (omnichannel).']
  redemption_count varchar [note: 'Current cumulative count of redemptions for this offer across all members. Updated in near-real-time from POS and OLO transaction feeds.']
  redemption_limit_per_member varchar [note: 'Maximum number of times a single loyalty member can redeem this offer during its active period. Null for unlimited redemptions.']
  stackable_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this offer can be combined with other offers in a single transaction. True = stackable, False = exclusive.']
  start_date date [note: 'Date when the offer becomes active and available for redemption by eligible members.']
  target_redemption_count varchar [note: 'Marketing team\'s target goal for total number of redemptions during the offer period. Used for campaign performance evaluation.']
  terms_and_conditions varchar [note: 'Legal terms and conditions governing the offer, including eligibility, restrictions, expiration, and disclaimers. Required for compliance with FTC advertising regulations.']
  total_redemption_limit decimal(18,2) [note: 'Maximum total number of redemptions allowed across all members for this offer (budget cap). Null for unlimited total redemptions.']

  Note: 'Master record for all personalized and mass loyalty offers distributed to members — targeted discounts, BOGO deals, bonus points events, LTO (Limited Time Offer) incentives, and gamification challenge rewards. Captures offer name, offer type (discount, bonus_points, free_item, challenge, sweepstakes), offer value, eligibility criteria (tier, segment, visit frequency), distribution channel (push notification, email, in-app, POS display), start/end dates, redemption limit per member, and offer status. Also owns member-level offer assignment detail: each assignment captures target member or segment, assignment channel, assignment timestamp, delivery status (sent, delivered, opened, clicked), member-specific expiry date, personalization flag, and engagement tracking. Sourced from Salesforce CRM campaign execution. Enables offer wallet management, delivery tracking, and distribution analytics.'
}

Table loyalty.offer_redemption {
  offer_redemption_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the offer redemption transaction. Primary key for the offer redemption record.']
  guest_order_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the order transaction associated with this offer redemption.']
  member_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the loyalty program member who redeemed the offer.']
  offer_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific loyalty offer that was redeemed.']
  pos_terminal_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the POS terminal or device where the redemption was processed. Applicable for in-store and drive-thru redemptions.']
  primary_offer_cashier_employee_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the employee who processed the redemption transaction at the POS. Null for digital channels.']
  restaurant_unit_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the restaurant location where the offer was redeemed.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this redemption record was first created in the data platform. Audit field for data lineage.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'Three-letter ISO 4217 currency code for the monetary amounts in this redemption transaction.']
  daypart varchar [note: 'Time-of-day segment when the offer was redeemed. Used to analyze redemption patterns by daypart and optimize offer targeting.']
  discount_amount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Monetary value of the discount applied to the order as a result of the offer redemption. Expressed in local currency.']
  discount_percentage decimal(5,2) [note: 'Percentage discount applied when discount_type is percentage. Null for non-percentage discount types.']
  discount_type varchar [note: 'Type of discount applied through the offer. Percentage for percent-off discounts, fixed_amount for dollar-off discounts, bogo for buy-one-get-one offers, free_item for complimentary items, combo_upgrade for meal upgrades, points_multiplier for accelerated points accrual.']
  final_order_amount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Total order amount after the offer discount was applied. Represents the actual amount paid by the member.']
  is_duplicate_attempt boolean [note: 'Boolean flag indicating whether this redemption was flagged as a duplicate attempt (member trying to redeem same offer multiple times).']
  is_first_redemption boolean [note: 'Boolean flag indicating whether this is the members first-ever offer redemption in the loyalty program. Used for new member engagement analytics.']
  member_tier varchar [note: 'Loyalty program tier of the member at the time of redemption. Captured for historical tracking of tier-specific redemption behavior.']
  offer_distribution_channel varchar [note: 'Channel through which the offer was originally distributed to the member. Distinct from redemption_channel which captures where it was redeemed. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: email|sms|push_notification|in_app|direct_mail|receipt_print|social_media — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  offer_expiration_date date [note: 'Date when the offer expires and can no longer be redeemed. Captured at redemption time for historical tracking.']
  original_order_amount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Total order amount before the offer discount was applied. Used to calculate discount impact and ACV (Average Check Value) lift.']
  points_earned varchar [note: 'Number of loyalty points earned by the member on this transaction after the offer discount was applied. May be zero if offer disqualifies points accrual.']
  points_multiplier_applied decimal(5,2) [note: 'Points multiplier applied to this transaction if the offer included accelerated points accrual (e.g., 2x points, 3x points). Default is 1.0 for standard accrual.']
  redemption_channel varchar [note: 'Channel through which the offer was redeemed. POS (Point of Sale) for in-store counter, OLO (Online Ordering) for web/app orders, drive_thru for drive-through lane, kiosk for self-service terminals, mobile_app for native app, third_party_delivery for 3PD (Third-Party Delivery) platforms.']
  redemption_code varchar [note: 'Unique alphanumeric code presented by the member to redeem the offer. May be system-generated or campaign-specific.']
  redemption_status varchar [note: 'Current status of the offer redemption. Fulfilled indicates successful redemption and discount applied, voided indicates redemption was reversed, duplicate_attempt indicates member tried to redeem same offer multiple times, expired indicates offer was past validity period, invalid indicates offer code was not recognized, pending indicates redemption is awaiting validation.']
  redemption_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the offer was redeemed by the member at the restaurant unit. Represents the business event time of the redemption transaction.']
  transaction_reference_number varchar [note: 'External transaction reference number from the POS or OLO system. Used for reconciliation and audit trail.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this redemption record was last modified in the data platform. Audit field for change tracking.']
  validation_method varchar [note: 'Method used to validate and apply the offer at redemption. Barcode_scan for scanning printed or digital barcodes, manual_entry for cashier-entered codes, qr_code for QR code scanning, nfc_tap for near-field communication, api_validation for system-to-system validation, loyalty_card_swipe for physical card swipe.']
  void_reason varchar [note: 'Free-text explanation for why the redemption was voided. Null if redemption was not voided.']
  void_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the redemption was voided. Null if redemption was not voided.']

  Note: 'Transactional record of every loyalty offer redeemed by a member at a restaurant unit. Captures member reference, offer reference, redemption channel (POS, OLO, drive-thru), restaurant unit, order reference, redemption timestamp, discount value applied, and redemption status (fulfilled, voided, duplicate_attempt). Distinct from reward redemption — offers are push-distributed incentives while rewards are pull-selected from the catalog.'
}

Table loyalty.program {
  program_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty program. Primary key.']
  brand_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to restaurant.brand. Business justification: A loyalty program is owned and operated by a specific brand. Brand governance, program P&L reporting, and franchise agreement compliance all require knowing which brand owns each program. The existing']
  birthday_bonus_points varchar [note: 'Number of bonus points awarded to members on their birthday. Zero if no birthday bonus is offered.']
  code varchar [note: 'Externally-known unique business identifier for the loyalty program used in integrations and reporting (e.g., REWARDS_PLUS, STAR_CLUB).']
  country_codes varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of ISO 3166-1 alpha-3 country codes where the program is available (e.g., USA,CAN,MEX). Null for global programs.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the program record was first created in the system.']
  currency_name varchar [note: 'Name of the loyalty currency used in the program (e.g., Stars, Points, Coins, Miles, Rewards).']
  description varchar [note: 'Detailed description of the loyalty program value proposition, benefits, and how it works. Used for internal reference and guest communications.']
  dollar_per_point decimal(10,4) [note: 'Monetary value of each loyalty point when redeemed. Used to calculate redemption value and liability.']
  end_date date [note: 'Date when the loyalty program was discontinued or sunset. Null for active programs.']
  enrollment_bonus_points varchar [note: 'Number of bonus points awarded to new members upon successful enrollment. Zero if no enrollment bonus is offered.']
  enrollment_channels varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of channels through which guests can enroll in the program (e.g., mobile_app, website, pos, kiosk, third_party).']
  gamification_enabled_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the program includes gamification elements such as challenges, badges, streaks, or missions.']
  geographic_scope varchar [note: 'Geographic coverage of the loyalty program: global (all markets), regional (multi-country region), country (single country), state (sub-national), or local (specific metro/franchise group).']
  launch_date date [note: 'Date when the loyalty program was officially launched and became available for guest enrollment.']
  minimum_redemption_points varchar [note: 'Minimum number of points required to make a redemption. Used to prevent micro-redemptions and manage transaction costs.']
  modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the program record was last modified in the system.']
  name varchar [note: 'Marketing name of the loyalty program displayed to guests (e.g., Rewards Plus, Star Club, VIP Circle).']
  olo_integration_enabled_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the program is integrated with online ordering platforms for digital points accrual and redemption.']
  ownership_model varchar [note: 'Ownership structure of the loyalty program: corporate (company-owned only), franchise (franchise-owned only), or hybrid (both corporate and franchise participation).']
  personalization_enabled_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the program uses guest data to deliver personalized offers, recommendations, and communications.']
  points_expiration_months decimal(9,4) [note: 'Number of months after which unused loyalty points expire. Null if points never expire.']
  points_per_dollar decimal(10,4) [note: 'Number of loyalty points earned per dollar spent. Used to calculate points accrual from transaction amounts.']
  pos_integration_enabled_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the program is integrated with POS systems for in-store points accrual and redemption.']
  privacy_policy_url varchar [note: 'Web URL to the privacy policy explaining how member data is collected, used, and protected.']
  program_status varchar [note: 'Current operational status of the loyalty program: active (accepting enrollments and transactions), inactive (not operational), suspended (temporarily paused), pilot (testing phase), or sunset (being phased out).']
  program_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the loyalty program structure: points-based (earn and redeem points), visit-based (frequency rewards), hybrid (combination), subscription (paid membership), or tiered (status levels).']
  referral_bonus_points varchar [note: 'Number of bonus points awarded to members who successfully refer a new member. Zero if no referral program exists.']
  restaurant_formats varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of restaurant formats where the program is valid (e.g., QSR, casual_dining, fine_dining, food_truck, ghost_kitchen).']
  subscription_fee_amount decimal(10,2) [note: 'Monthly or annual subscription fee required for paid membership programs. Null for free programs.']
  subscription_fee_frequency decimal(18,2) [note: 'Billing frequency for subscription-based programs: monthly, annual, or one-time. Null for free programs.']
  target_audience varchar [note: 'Description of the primary guest segment the program is designed to attract and retain (e.g., frequent diners, families, business travelers, value seekers).']
  terms_and_conditions_url varchar [note: 'Web URL to the official terms and conditions document governing the loyalty program.']
  third_party_delivery_enabled_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the program supports points accrual and redemption through third-party delivery platforms.']
  tier_enabled_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the program includes membership tiers with progressive benefits (True) or is a single-tier program (False).']

  Note: 'Master configuration record for each loyalty program operated by Restaurants — covering program name, program type (points-based, visit-based, hybrid, subscription), currency name (e.g., \'Stars\', \'Points\', \'Coins\'), points-to-dollar conversion rate, program launch date, geographic scope (global, regional, country), applicable restaurant formats (QSR, casual, fine-dining), enrollment channels, and program status. Supports multi-program architectures across franchise and company-owned units.'
}

Table loyalty.enrollment_event {
  enrollment_event_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty program enrollment event. Primary key for the enrollment event transaction.']
  initial_tier_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the membership tier assigned at enrollment. Typically the base tier for new members, but may be elevated tier for transfer or upgrade enrollments.']
  primary_enrollment_member_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the loyalty program member who enrolled. Links to the member master record.']
  primary_enrollment_restaurant_unit_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the restaurant unit where the enrollment occurred. Null for digital-only enrollments without a specific unit association.']
  primary_enrollment_staff_employee_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the staff member who assisted with the enrollment. Null for self-service enrollments. Used for staff performance tracking.']
  primary_enrollment_transaction_guest_order_id varchar [note: 'Original transaction identifier from the source system. Used for reconciliation and traceability back to the source system.']
  program_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the loyalty program the member enrolled in. Supports multi-program environments.']
  welcome_offer_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific welcome offer or promotional reward issued at enrollment. Null if no offer was issued.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this enrollment event record was first created in the data platform. System audit field for data lineage.']
  email_opt_in_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member opted in to receive email communications at enrollment. Required for CAN-SPAM compliance.']
  enrollment_channel varchar [note: 'Channel through which the enrollment occurred. OLO (Online Ordering) for web/app orders, POS (Point of Sale) for in-restaurant, mobile_app for native app, kiosk for self-service terminals, staff_assisted for employee-facilitated, web for website.']
  enrollment_country_code varchar [note: 'Country where the enrollment occurred. ISO 3166-1 alpha-3 three-letter country codes. Used for geographic segmentation and compliance. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: USA|CAN|MEX|GBR|FRA|DEU|AUS|JPN|CHN|BRA — 10 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  enrollment_device_type varchar [note: 'Type of device used to complete the enrollment. Supports channel and user experience analysis.']
  enrollment_geolocation varchar [note: 'Geographic coordinates (latitude, longitude) of the enrollment location if captured. Format: latitude,longitude. Used for location-based analytics.']
  enrollment_ip_address varchar [note: 'IP address from which the enrollment was initiated. Used for fraud detection and geographic analysis. May be considered PII in some jurisdictions.']
  enrollment_language varchar [note: 'Language preference selected by the member at enrollment. ISO 639-2 three-letter language codes. Used for personalized communications. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: eng|spa|fra|deu|ita|por|zho|jpn|kor — 9 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  enrollment_notes varchar [note: 'Free-text notes or comments about the enrollment event. Used for special circumstances, exceptions, or customer service annotations.']
  enrollment_number varchar [note: 'Business-facing unique enrollment transaction number. Format: ENR followed by 10 digits. Used for customer service and audit tracking.']
  enrollment_source_system varchar [note: 'Name of the source system that captured the enrollment event. Examples: Olo, Oracle MICROS, Salesforce CRM, Mobile App. Used for data lineage and troubleshooting.']
  enrollment_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the enrollment event. Completed indicates successful enrollment; pending indicates awaiting verification; failed indicates enrollment did not complete; cancelled indicates member-initiated cancellation; reversed indicates system or compliance reversal.']
  enrollment_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the enrollment event occurred in the source system. Represents the real-world business event time, distinct from record audit timestamps.']
  enrollment_type varchar [note: 'Type of enrollment action. New indicates first-time enrollment; re_enrollment indicates returning member; transfer indicates program migration; upgrade indicates tier promotion enrollment.']
  fraud_check_status varchar [note: 'Status of fraud detection checks performed at enrollment. Passed indicates clean enrollment; failed indicates suspected fraud; pending indicates checks in progress; not_required indicates no checks were performed.']
  fraud_score decimal(5,2) [note: 'Numeric fraud risk score assigned to the enrollment event by fraud detection systems. Range typically 0-100, with higher scores indicating higher risk. Null if fraud checking was not performed.']
  initial_points_awarded varchar [note: 'Number of loyalty points awarded to the member at enrollment as a sign-up bonus. Zero if no points were awarded.']
  marketing_opt_in_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member opted in to receive marketing communications at enrollment. True if opted in; False if declined.']
  push_notification_opt_in_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member opted in to receive mobile app push notifications at enrollment.']
  referral_code varchar [note: 'Specific referral or campaign code used during enrollment. Enables attribution tracking for member-get-member programs and promotional campaigns.']
  referral_source varchar [note: 'Source that drove the enrollment. Organic for unprompted; referral_code for member referral; campaign for marketing campaign; social_media for social channels; email for email marketing; in_store for restaurant promotion; partner for third-party partner. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: organic|referral_code|campaign|social_media|email|in_store|partner — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  sms_opt_in_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member opted in to receive SMS/text message communications at enrollment. Required for TCPA compliance.']
  terms_accepted_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member accepted the loyalty program terms and conditions at enrollment. Required for compliance and legal purposes.']
  terms_version varchar [note: 'Version identifier of the terms and conditions accepted by the member at enrollment. Enables tracking of which terms version the member agreed to.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this enrollment event record was last modified in the data platform. System audit field for change tracking.']
  verification_completed_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether required verification has been completed. True if completed; False if pending or not completed.']
  verification_completed_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when enrollment verification was completed. Null if verification is not required or not yet completed.']
  verification_required_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the enrollment requires additional verification (e.g., email verification, identity verification). True if verification is required; False if not required.']
  welcome_offer_issued_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether a welcome offer or sign-up bonus was issued to the member upon enrollment. True if issued; False if not issued.']

  Note: 'Transactional record of every loyalty program enrollment action — new enrollments, re-enrollments, and program transfers. Captures member reference, program reference, enrollment channel (OLO, POS, in-app, kiosk, staff-assisted), enrollment restaurant unit, enrollment timestamp, referral source (organic, referral_code, campaign), welcome offer issued flag, and enrollment status. Feeds acquisition funnel analysis and channel attribution for the loyalty program.'
}

Table loyalty.offer_distribution {
  offer_distribution_id varchar [pk, note: 'Primary key for the offer_distribution association']
  member_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to the loyalty member who received the offer distribution.']
  offer_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to the loyalty offer that was distributed to the member.']
  channel varchar [note: 'The specific channel through which this offer was distributed to this member. May differ from the offer-level distribution_channel when personalized channel routing is applied. Sourced from detection phase distribution_channel and offer description assignment_channel.']
  distributed_at timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the offer was distributed (sent) to the member. Marks the start of the distribution lifecycle. Sourced from detection phase distribution_date.']
  distribution_channel varchar [note: 'Primary channel through which the offer is communicated to members: push_notification, email, in_app (mobile app banner), sms, pos_display (printed receipt or screen), direct_mail. [Moved from offer: The offer-level distribution_channel captures the primary/default channel for the offer campaign. However, the per-member assignment channel (which may be personalized) belongs to the offer_distribution association. The offer master should retain distribution_channel as the campaign-level default; the association captures the actual per-member delivery channel.]']
  is_viewed boolean [note: 'Flag indicating whether the member has viewed (opened) this offer in their offer wallet or via the delivery channel. Sourced directly from detection phase is_viewed_flag.']
  member_expiry_date date [note: 'Member-specific expiration date for this offer assignment. May differ from the offer-level end_date due to personalized expiry windows. Sourced from detection phase expiration_date and offer description member-level expiry.']
  personalization_score decimal [note: 'Numeric score representing the degree of personalization applied to this specific offer-member assignment, used for targeting model evaluation and A/B testing. Sourced directly from detection phase personalization_score.']
  personalized_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this offer is personalized to individual members based on purchase history and preferences (True) or is a mass offer distributed to all eligible members (False). [Moved from offer: This boolean on the offer master indicates whether the offer is personalization-eligible at the campaign level. The actual per-member personalization score and personalization state belong to the offer_distribution association record, not the offer master. The offer master flag can be retained as a campaign-level indicator, but the per-member personalization detail moves to the association.]']
  redeemed_at timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the member redeemed this specific offer distribution. Null if not yet redeemed. Belongs to the distribution record, not the offer master.']
  redemption_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of this specific offer-member distribution record. Tracks the full funnel from distribution through redemption or expiry. Sourced directly from detection phase redemption_status and offer description delivery_status.']

  Note: 'This association product represents the Distribution Event between a loyalty offer and a loyalty member. It captures the full lifecycle of a single offer being assigned and delivered to a specific member — from initial distribution through delivery, engagement, and final redemption or expiry. Each record links one offer to one member and carries attributes that exist only in the context of that specific offer-member assignment: when it was sent, through which channel, whether the member viewed it, its member-specific expiry, and its current redemption status. This is the operational record that powers the member offer wallet, delivery tracking, and redemption lift analytics. Sourced from Salesforce CRM campaign execution.. Existence Justification: In restaurant loyalty operations, the marketing team actively distributes specific offers to specific members as a first-class business process — this is not derivable from redemption data alone. An offer can be distributed to thousands of members, and a member can hold multiple active offers in their \'offer wallet\' simultaneously. The distribution event (offer sent → delivered → viewed → redeemed/expired) has its own lifecycle, attributes, and business name (\'offer distribution\' or \'member offer assignment\') that neither the offer master nor the member master can capture.'
}
